# About this item

- ONLY ONE INGREDIENT: 100% Pure Micronized Creatine Monohydrate. Vegan, Non-GMO, Soy Free and Gluten Free.
- HIGHEST QUALITY: Naked Creatine is the highest grade creatine monohydrate supplement available.
- FAST DISSOLVING: Unlike other brands, Naked Creatine dissolves quickly in water or your juice of choice.
- RAPID ABSORPTION: Pure creatine monohydrate allows for fast absorption which enhances gains, strength, and increases training capacity.
- NO ADDITIVES: Made from pure monohydrate creatine with no artificial sweeteners, flavors or colors.

### Product Safety and Compliance DetailsProduct Safety and Compliance Details

### Safe use

As the [Food and Drug Administration (FDA)](https://www.fda.gov/media/158337/download?attachment) advises, dietary supplements can support your overall health but may also have powerful effects on the body. It’s important to read labels carefully, exercise caution, and consult your healthcare professional before taking any supplement. Side effects are more likely if supplements are taken in high doses, as substitutes for prescribed medications, or in combination with multiple supplements. If you experience severe side effects, discontinue use immediately and seek medical attention.

### LEGAL DISCLAIMER

Some states prohibit the sale of products intended for weight loss or muscle building to individuals under age 18. Check your local laws prior to purchase.

How customer reviews and ratings work

Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

Amazon Customer

_5 out of 5 stars_

##### One Ingredient, Zero Side Effects and USA-Made!

I purchased the NAKED Pure Micronized Creatine Monohydrate because it is supposed to help memory. It was a bigger container than I was expecting. It had safety sealing on both the outside and inside. I "loaded" the first 3 days by taking it three times a day. Now I take it once a day. It dissolves easily in water, but now I put it in my breakfast smoothie when I make it. I didn't notice any bad smell, taste, after-taste, upset stomach or any other adverse side effects. It comes with a long-handled scoop for the proper amount. I like that it is only one ingredient, non-GMO, gluten free and made in the USA. The only problem I have is once in a while I get the lid on too tight and since the container is so big around it is kind of hard to get my hand around to get it loose. Good value for the money and I will buy this product again.

🏋️‍♂️ Performance: Within the first 10–14 days, I noticed better endurance and strength during workouts. My muscles feel fuller, and I recover faster between sets.

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ One Ingredient, Zero Side Effects and USA-Made!](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R2IWN493EQRI8G/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

I purchased the NAKED Pure Micronized Creatine Monohydrate because it is supposed to help memory.

It was a bigger container than I was expecting. It had safety sealing on both the outside and inside.

I "loaded" the first 3 days by taking it three times a day. Now I take it once a day.

It dissolves easily in water, but now I put it in my breakfast smoothie when I make it.

I didn't notice any bad smell, taste, after-taste, upset stomach or any other adverse side effects.

It comes with a long-handled scoop for the proper amount.

I like that it is only one ingredient, non-GMO, gluten free and made in the USA.

The only problem I have is once in a while I get the lid on too tight and since the container is so big around it is kind of hard to get my hand around to get it loose.

Good value for the money and I will buy this product again.

##### One Ingredient, Zero Side Effects and USA-Made!










Reviewed in the United States on July 19, 2025







I purchased the NAKED Pure Micronized Creatine Monohydrate because it is supposed to help memory.

It was a bigger container than I was expecting. It had safety sealing on both the outside and inside.

I "loaded" the first 3 days by taking it three times a day. Now I take it once a day.

It dissolves easily in water, but now I put it in my breakfast smoothie when I make it.

I didn't notice any bad smell, taste, after-taste, upset stomach or any other adverse side effects.

It comes with a long-handled scoop for the proper amount.

I like that it is only one ingredient, non-GMO, gluten free and made in the USA.

The only problem I have is once in a while I get the lid on too tight and since the container is so big around it is kind of hard to get my hand around to get it loose.

Good value for the money and I will buy this product again.

It was my first time i every used creatine and i was scared because there are a lot of fake products but after searching for a while i finally ordered this product. In first week i didn't notice any change in my body but after 2-3 weeks now it started working. Usually the next day after workout my muscle used to be very sore and used to pain when i touch them but now after using it my muscle recover very fast and i feel very less soreness and now my muscle also don't pain while touching. Good product but i guess there should be flavored options too because unflavored creatine taste a little chalky.
